## 逐条摘录

### 1. Technological Change and the Stock Market

- PDF：[000282803769206287.pdf.pdf](./000282803769206287.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：*（AER期刊，无独立关键词栏）*

**同段完整语句：**

The embodiment assumption is familiar from Robert M. Solow (1960). Recent studies find a significant role for embodied change in growth. Jeremy Greenwood et al. (1997) estimate that embodied technical progress in equipment alone contributed 60 percent to overall Total Factor Productivity (TFP) change in the United States from 1954 to 1990; Michael Gort et al. (1999) argue that embodied progress is very important for structures too.

### 2. Technological Change and the Stock Market

- PDF：[000282803769206287.pdf.pdf](./000282803769206287.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：18
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：*（AER期刊，无独立关键词栏）*

**同段完整语句：**

Gort et al. (1999) employ similar ideas to study structures. They use a vintage capital framework, with continuous technical progress, to derive an analog of equation (17); measure d# with data on building rents by age; derive d from maintenance expenditures; and then back out a rate of technical change. Greenwood et al. (1997) use a continuous-time version of (17) to relate the rate of embodied technical change to the rate of decline in the quality-adjusted price of new investment goods relative to consumption.

### 3. Measuring embodied technical change in the US local telephone industry

- PDF：[00036840010025100.pdf.pdf](./00036840010025100.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：*（未见独立关键词）*

**同段完整语句：**

Hulten (1992) uses the estimates of quality change obtained from the price literature in line with conventional growth accounting. He measures unobserved embodiment parameters using the ratio of the Bureau of Labor Statistics (BLS) quality-unadjusted price indexes to Gordon's (1990) quality-adjusted price indexes. Greenwood et al. (1997) take a general equilibrium approach to disentangle investment-specific technological change from the more traditional Hicks-neutral form of technological progress. Gort et al. (1993) take advantage of plant panel data, which overcomes several data problems of previous studies, to estimate the vintage effect of additions to capital within the framework of a production function.

### 4. Productive physical investment and growth: testing the validity of the AK model from a panel perspective

- PDF：[00036840701335611.pdf.pdf](./00036840701335611.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：14
- 类型：模型设定 / 资本品部门
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：*（未见独立关键词）*

**同段完整语句：**

Furthermore, our results lend support to endogenous growth models, where productive investment appears to be the engine of growth. These high social returns associated with productive investment and in particular with investment in producer durables may be attributed to the presence of positive externalities to the accumulation of productive capital (Romer, 1986), to the process of technological transfer through trade of capital goods across countries (Eaton and Kortum, 2006) and to embodiment of technological progress in new vintages of capital (Greenwood et al., 1997). It can also be due to the existence of learning by doing processes in the accumulation of physical capital as in Arrow (1962). In this study, we do not pursue further, which of these mechanisms are the ones that lead to such high social rates of return to productive capital, hence preventing the economy from entering into the area of diminishing returns as in the neoclassical paradigm.

### 5. Technology and spillovers: evidence from Indian manufacturing microdata

- PDF：[00036840802600301.pdf.pdf](./00036840802600301.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：*（未见独立关键词）*

**同段完整语句：**

I. Introduction Discussion of the positive effects of investment in machinery and R&D on a firm's productivity is reasonably extensive in economic theory. Nelson (1964) and Greenwood et al. (1997), among others, argue that machinery of a relatively new vintage embodies the latest technology, and therefore, fosters higher labour productivity growth. Meanwhile, King and Robson (1993) argue that investment in machinery generates significant learning effects which spill over to other firms. Furthermore, Romer (1986) stresses investment in R&D as an engine of long-run growth, while Griliches (1979) highlights the favourable impact of spillovers from such investments.

### 6. Testing the technology interpretation of news shocks

- PDF：[00036846.2011.566209.pdf.pdf](./00036846.2011.566209.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：1
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：business cycles; news

**同段完整语句：**

by suggesting that technology shocks might not take the form of surprise shocks to Total Factor Productivity (TFP), the workhorse of most RBC models. Fisher (2003), following Greenwood et al. (1997), distinguishes between shocks to disembodied and embodied technology. He finds the former to be unimportant indeed, but claims that shocks to Investment Specific Technology (IST) are the major source of hours' variance. Simultaneously, Beaudry and Portier (2006) suggest expectational shocks reflecting news about future technological developments as an important force behind macro fluctuations.

### 7. China's catch-up to the US economy: decomposing TFP through investment-specific technology and human capital

- PDF：[00036846.2014.948677.pdf.pdf](./00036846.2014.948677.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：3
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：China; investment-specific technology; human capital; convergence

**同段完整语句：**

In the late 1980s and 1990s, the IST literature moved beyond the development of embodied technology theory and focused on the role of IST in advanced economies, particularly the United States, analysing the productivity slowdown starting in the early 1970s (Baily et al., 1988; Hulten, 1992; Greenwood et al., 1997, 2000; Gordon, 2007). These authors observe a strong negative correlation over time between the quality and price of capital. Thus, the quality-adjusted price of investment reflects the current technological state of investment, and its inverse is used to measure IST. In the 1990s, US productivity gained strength after declining in the 1980s, and the role IST played in this revival was subsequently studied by Cummins and Violante (2002), Sakellaris and Wilson (2004) and Fisher (2006).

### 8. China's catch-up to the US economy: decomposing TFP through investment-specific technology and human capital

- PDF：[00036846.2014.948677.pdf.pdf](./00036846.2014.948677.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：3
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：China; investment-specific technology; human capital; convergence

**同段完整语句：**

However, this price does not necessarily reflect the increase in efficiency and higher quality of equipment as technology improves over time. Gordon (2007) measures the quality bias in National Income and Product Accounts' equipment price data for the period 1947–1983 to quantify the impact of IST on the US economy. Greenwood et al. (1997) and Cummins and Violante (2002) extended the quality-adjusted price index to 1992 and 2000, respectively. The quality bias – the ratio of the quality-adjusted to the unadjusted price index – estimated in these studies has a strong negative trend through the end of the sample, as depicted in Fig. 2, indicating continuous and steady improvements in the quality of equipment over time. Accounting for this quality bias, allows us to identify changes in IST for the United States.

### 9. China's catch-up to the US economy: decomposing TFP through investment-specific technology and human capital

Using their data, we calculated the annualized growth rate for each 5-year period by employing the standard growth formula $h_{t+1} = (1 + g_h)h_t$ to generate yearly data for the period 1952-2009. Following Hall and Jones (1999), we assume that the conversion parameter for schooling ($\psi$) is 0.1. We define the physical capital share as $\alpha = 0.33$ as in Greenwood et al. (1997) and Hall and Jones (1999). Our main data source for IST is Cummins and Violante (2002). For the United States, IST is defined as one over the quality-adjusted price index $P_H^U$ deflated by the consumption price index $CI^U$, that is, $\tau_U = 1/p_H^U$, where $p_H^U=(P_H^U/CI^U)$.

### 11. China's catch-up to the US economy: decomposing TFP through investment-specific technology and human capital

- PDF：[00036846.2014.948677.pdf.pdf](./00036846.2014.948677.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：8
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：China; investment-specific technology; human capital; convergence

**同段完整语句：**

This indicates that, in the United States, both human capital and IST explain a large portion of the residual TFP together and individually. Changing the baseline to Step 2 (the model with human capital) and comparing TFP to that in Step 3, IST captures an additional 61.72% and 46.30% of TFP for the first and second period, respectively. Although our numbers are not directly comparable to Greenwood et al. (1997), who found that IST explains about 58% of all output growth for the period 1954–1990, the results of both the studies are similar insofar as IST explains a significant portion of the growth of the economy. Figure 7(a) details the Chinese TFP decomposition using $\tau_{IC}$ for the period 1952–2000 and Fig. 7(b) decomposes the Chinese TFP using $\tau_{EC}$ for the period 1976–2000. Our calculation and the historical account tell a parallel story: starting at the end of the 1970s, China's economy, as measured through TFP, entered a period of sustained growth that is still continuing, and this growth is robust to the effects of human capital; however, after IST is accounted for the growth in TFP abated.

### 12. Structural Transformation of India: A Quantitative Analysis

- PDF：[0019466219858852.pdf.pdf](./0019466219858852.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：9
- 类型：模型设定 / 资本品部门

- 关键词：Structural transformation, elasticity of substitution, manufacturing, services, productivity growth

**同段完整语句：**

For example, software currently is both a sizeable and increasing component of investment in the US economy, and that most software innovation takes place in the service sector (Herrendorf et al., 2014). This is most likely true in the Indian case as well where the services sector dominates and specifically the rise of the information technology has been at the heart of it. On the other hand, Herrendorf et al. (2014) consider a separate investment sector that allows different rates of technological progress in the investment sector as the literature on investment-specific technical progress suggests (e.g., Greenwood, Hercowitz, & Krusell, 1997). However, adding one more sector for investment also raises the issue of how the output of investment is allocated across the three broad sectors while taking the model to the data. To simplify the matters, we assume that the final goods sector contributes for both the consumption and investment.

### 13. The Rise of the Skill Premium in Mexican Maquiladoras

- PDF：[00220380802265272.pdf.pdf](./00220380802265272.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：5
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：skill premium, maquiladoras, wage differentials, skill-biased technical change, capital-skill complementarity

**同段完整语句：**

Our aim, in the context of evidence for Mexico, is to enhance our understanding of how relative wages in an export-oriented sector respond to increases in global fragmentation of production in at least two ways. First, there is the motivation of applying a theoretical framework of SBTC to Mexico's export-oriented sector under increasingly global fragmentation of production. Using monthly data from Mexican maquiladoras' from 1990–2006, our research strategy compares the basic Katz and Murphy (1992) model to Acemoglu (2002), who takes into account the complementarity between skilled labour and capital. The main idea dates to Greenwood et al. (1997) through the introduction of new and more efficient capital goods as an important source of US productivity change. Technological advances have made equipment less expensive, triggering increases in the accumulation of equipment both in the short and long run. Krusell et al. (2000) hypothesise that capital-skill complementarity may be important for understanding wage inequality, because the stock of equipment has been growing at a very high rate in recent years.

### 14. Does democratization lower consumer prices? Regime type, prices, and the consumer–producer tradeoff

- PDF：[0192512117731264.pdf.pdf](./0192512117731264.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：8
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：Democratization, regime type, prices, consumer–producer tradeoff

**同段完整语句：**

Inclusion of year-fixed effects is also essential, although for a more technical reason. Changes in the consumer advantage ratio in a country can occur if the global cost of consumption goods rises more slowly or rapidly than that of investment goods in any given year. Shifts of this nature occur all the time due to commodity-price or innovation shocks and, in fact, there has been a worldwide trend of less expensive capital goods since 1950 due to technological advance (Greenwood et al., 1997). Year-fixed effects soak up changes in relative prices that have nothing to do with domestic politics and economics in a given country. Finally, we include a few other control variables.

They demonstrated that lifting constraint inequalities leads to a singular harvesting control. Their use of generalized functions simplifies the analysis. We here treat the optimal management of age-distributed capital investments, which is a vintage capital problem (Cooley et al., 1997; Greenwood et al., 1997; Boucekkine et al., 2010; Jovanovic and Yatsenko, 2012). Goetz et al. (2008) proved the bang-bang structure of age-structured investment control in a vintage model governed by a Lotka-McKendrik model. Our objective functional is nonlinear; the process is different; and the outcomes differ from those of Goetz et al. (2008) and Hritonenko and Yatsenko (2012).

### 17. Probing into the social layers of entrepreneurship: outlines of the sociology of enterprise

- PDF：[089856299283155.pdf.pdf](./089856299283155.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：8
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：entrepreneurship, sociology of enterprise, social layers, economic sociology

**同段完整语句：**

Moreover, from the 'socio-structuring' perspective on entrepreneurship and development the mystery of the Solow residual in mainstream economics is not greatly alleviated by taking it (as in real business-cycle models) as a direct measure of technological progress or technologically-induced productivity growth. This latter is an exogenous variable in the standard neoclassical model, especially the Cobb-Douglas production function, that includes only labour and capital inputs as explanatory variables (Dougherty and Jorgenson 1996). For example, some economists (Greenwood et al. 1997: 343–4) argue that '60% of postwar productivity growth can be attributed to investment-specific technological change', i.e. to the residual thus interpreted. However others (Rotemberg and Woodford 1996) complain that Solow residuals might not be a 'good measure' of productivity growth because of various reasons, such as imperfect competition, overhead costs, unmeasured variation in factor utilization, etc. Hence they argue that the evidence for little residual autocorrelation justifies a 'random-walk specification' in methodological terms, i.e. viewing the underlying variables measured by the residual as stochastic ones. This is in conflict with large autocorrelation in the output growth, and thus suggests that it is implausible modelling the latter as a random-walk.

**同段完整语句：**

Unless otherwise indicated, capital will hereafter refer to productive capital as defined above. Greenwood et al. (1997) and Hornstein & Krusell (1996) are prominent examples of the price approach to quantifying embodied technological change. This price-side literature uses the growth rate in the relative price of investment (to consumption) to infer the rate of embodied technological change. For this approach to be valid, the relative price must fully and accurately account for quality improvements in investment (capital) goods.

### 22. The sources of total factor productivity growth: Evidence from Canadian data

- PDF：[10438590410001629007.pdf.pdf](./10438590410001629007.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：3
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：Investment-specific technological change, Total factor productivity, Economic growth

**同段完整语句：**

The time path of IST was tracked using movements in the relative price of equipment. Between 1961 and 1996 the price of new equipment relative to the price of consumer non-durables and services declined by approximately 4.0 per year, while the rate of investment in equipment rose by 4.0 percent per year. This negative co-movement has been interpreted in the literature as evidence of IST (see Greenwood et al. 1997, 2000 and Dunaway et al. 2000). Time series for TFP and RNT were calculated from Canadian data using parameter values derived from a Real Business Cycle (RBC) model that was calibrated to the Canadian economy.

For example, the relevant real business cycle (RBC) literature (see Greenwood, Hercowitz and Krusell 1997; 2000) has focused on measuring the effects of IST and RNT on labor productivity.

### 25. The sources of total factor productivity growth: Evidence from Canadian data

- PDF：[10438590410001629007.pdf.pdf](./10438590410001629007.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：5

- 关键词：Investment-specific technological change, Total factor productivity, Economic growth

**同段完整语句：**

In this section a model of the Canadian economy is described, which will help to identify appropriate methods for calculating time series estimates of technology and productivity and for isolating the contributions of RNT and IST to TFP. The model described is a version of the RBC model constructed by Greenwood et al. (1997), and used by Greenwood et al. (1997; 2000) for measuring the impact of IST and RNT on the rate of labor productivity growth in the U.S. economy. This particular version of the RBC model allows for new equipment to become increasingly more efficient with the passage of time.

### 27. Evaluating the effects of investment in information and communication technology

- PDF：[10438599.2011.561998.pdf.pdf](./10438599.2011.561998.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：information and communication technology, productivity, labour productivity, ICT investment

**同段完整语句：**

Introduction The analysis of the impact of information and communication technology (ICT) has long been the subject of a vast and growing literature, mainly from the end of the 1990s onwards. Most of the studies have been focused on the effects of ICT investment on the US aggregate output and labour productivity growth. Thus, for example, Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997) reported that approximately 60% of the US postwar productivity growth (long-term growth) can be attributed to investment-specific technological change. Three years later, the same authors (Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell 2000) focused on the short run, and found that this technological change contributed relatively less to the US business cycle (only about 30%) than to the long-term growth. Likewise, Jorgenson and Stiroh (2000), Oliner and Sichel (2000, 2003), Jorgenson (2001), Pakko (2002), Jorgenson, Ho, and Stiroh (2003) and several others concluded that ICT has contributed to faster gross domestic product (GDP) and labour productivity growth in the USA from the second half

### 28. Evaluating the effects of investment in information and communication technology

- PDF：[10438599.2011.561998.pdf.pdf](./10438599.2011.561998.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：3
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：information and communication technology, productivity, labour productivity, ICT investment

**同段完整语句：**

The main limitation of this approach is that such decompositions are only possible on the basis of certain assumptions (cost-minimizing producers, competitive factor markets, well-measured input and output, and constant returns to scale), which are unlikely to be fully satisfied. This approach, however, provides a simple and consistent method which can be used as a starting point to identify the contribution of the various inputs to aggregate growth, and thus to derive the relative importance of ICT to economic growth. The second strand – exemplified by the research of Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997) – is based on dynamic general equilibrium (DGE) models (see also Bakhshi and Larsen 2005; Carlaw and Kosempel 2004; Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell 2000; Kiley 2001; Martínez, Rodríguez, and Torres 2008; Pakko 2002, among others). The DGE models are firmly grounded in economic theory and do not attempt historical decompositions of aggregate growth (as the growth accounting approach does), but instead, quantify the contribution to growth of specific technological change. The key advantage of the DGE approach over the growth accounting methodology, according to Bakhshi and Larsen (2005), is that the macroeconomic implications of a shock to investment-specific technological progress can be simulated in a forward-looking environment.

The properties of the balanced growth path are generalized by recent growth models as in Greenwood et al. (1997) and Fisher (2006), which deal with a more complex case that the degree of technological progress is different among various sectors of the economy. These studies show that the ratio of nominal consumption to nominal output or the ratio of nominal investment to nominal output becomes stable when the rate of technological change is different between consumption goods and investment goods. Kim (2009) extends the model to an environment in which the degree of technological progress is different between the manufacturing and service sectors.

### 34. Unemployment vs. Mismatch of Talents: Reconsidering Unemployment Benefits

- PDF：[1468-0297.00432.pdf.pdf](./1468-0297.00432.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：3
- 类型：投资特定技术冲击 / 商业周期
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：unemployment, search-matching, skilled-biased technological change, wage inequality, labour market

**同段完整语句：**

Our basic idea is that economies which are in all identical except for the replacement ratio may react very differently to the occurrence of a common technological shock, which enhances the importance of mismatch. We argue that this mismatch-biased shock is related to what other papers have referred to as skill-biased technical change. To see the source of the similarity, we refer to the observation of Greenwood et al. (1997), for the United States, who show that, starting in the mid 1970's, there is an acceleration of investment-specific technological change, associated with a fall in the price of capital relative to that of labour. Such technological change has been called skilled-biased technological change, and is consistent with postulating a relation of complementarity between capital and skilled labour (see Krusell et al., 1995). In this paper, motivated by the evidence discussed above about the increase of earning instability and within group wage inequality, we postulate that there also exists a relation of complementarity between capital and capital-specific-skills (see Violante (1997) for a similar notation of technical change in a model where workers' skills are technology-specific).

The weights of factor inputs in the calculation of the MFP growth residual should correspond to the marginal productivity of labour and capital. These are not observable and we followed the standard procedure of proxying them with income shares, which can be easily computed from national accounts. This corresponds to making a few assumptions, most importantly that the product and input markets are perfectly competitive and that there are constant returns to scale (Morrison, 1999).

### 38. Managing technological innovation: China's strategy and challenges

- PDF：[17468771011086238.pdf.pdf](./17468771011086238.pdf.pdf)

**同段完整语句：**

The US Department of Commerce (2000b) has pointed out that all forms of economic development are based upon well-conceived and executed programs to strengthen and expand the science and technology (S&T) resources of a state. ### 39. The impact of firm size on dynamic incentives and investment

- PDF：[1756-2171.12171.pdf.pdf](./1756-2171.12171.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：6
- 类型：文献定位 / 简短引用
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：firm size, dynamic incentives, investment, moral hazard, principal-agent

**同段完整语句：**

To formulate this path, we adopt a simple capital accumulation model in which the firm's capital stock accumulates by investment $dI_t$, where $I_t$ denotes the cumulative investment up to time $t$ with $I_0 = 0$, but depreciates at a rate of $\delta \in [0, 1)$. That is, $k_t$ evolves according to $dk_t = dI_t - \delta k_t \, dt$. Also, as is standard in the capital accumulation model (e.g., Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell, 1997), instantaneous investment $dI_t$ is determined by the remaining output after paying pecuniary compensations to both parties. We thereby provide a unified framework in which the agent's incentive scheme and the corporate growth path are simultaneously determined by a simple contract. Combining with the output process laid in (1), we obtain the following stochastic differential equation (SDE) of $k_t$:

$$
dk_t = dY_t - (c_t + d_t)dt - \delta k_t \, dt = [f(k_t, e_t) - c_t - d_t - \delta k_t]dt + \sigma k_t \, dW_t = dI_t
$$

### 40. The micro elasticity of substitution and non-neutral technology

- PDF：[1756-2171.12265.pdf.pdf](./1756-2171.12265.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：1
- 类型：模型设定 / 资本品部门
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：elasticity of substitution, capital-labor, non-neutral technology, manufacturing plants

**同段完整语句：**

The elasticity of substitution between capital and labor is central for several policy questions in economics. It determines how firms' usage of labor and capital respond to policy changes that affect factor prices, such as investment subsidies (Hall and Jorgenson, 1967); tariffs on capital goods (Cai, Ravikumar, and Riezman, 2015); changes in trade barriers (Dornbusch, Fischer, and Samuelson, 1980); minimum wages (Aaronson and French, 2007); and firing costs (Petrin and Sivadasan, 2013). The elasticity is also important to understand both some of the reasons why firms innovate (Acemoglu, 2010), as well as how technological change affects relative factor intensities, either through nonneutral productivity (Hicks, 1932; Sato, 1975), or investment-specific technical change (Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell, 1997).

### 54. Investment Shocks and Asset Prices

- PDF：[662221.pdf.pdf](./662221.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：5
- 类型：模型设定 / 资本品部门
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：investment shocks, asset prices, risk premia, investment-specific technology

**同段完整语句：**

Gomes et al. use a general equilibrium model with productivity shocks and study firms that produce durable and nondurable consumption goods. I use a model that has productivity shocks as well as investment shocks and study firms that produce consumption and investment goods. Investment-specific technology shocks have become a standard feature of real business cycle models (Solow 1960; Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell 1997, 2000; Fisher 2006). Greenwood et al. (1997) use the price of new equipment as an empirical measure of the investment shock and argue that such shocks are important determinants of long-run growth. Fisher reaches similar conclusions by identifying the investment shock through long-run restrictions in a vector autoregression.

### 55. Investment Shocks and Asset Prices

- PDF：[662221.pdf.pdf](./662221.pdf.pdf)

**同段完整语句：**

I use a model that has productivity shocks as well as investment shocks and study firms that produce consumption and investment goods. Investment-specific technology shocks have become a standard feature of real business cycle models (Solow 1960; Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell 1997, 2000; Fisher 2006). Greenwood et al. (1997) use the price of new equipment as an empirical measure of the investment shock and argue that such shocks are important determinants of long-run growth. Fisher reaches similar conclusions by identifying the investment shock through long-run restrictions in a vector autoregression. I contribute to this literature by showing how financial data can be useful in measuring investment shocks.

### 59. aer.100.1.164.pdf

- PDF：[aer.100.1.164.pdf.pdf](./aer.100.1.164.pdf.pdf)

**同段完整语句：**

In a survey of entry and exit, Geroski (1995) reports little success relating differences in turnover rates to industry characteristics, mostly measures of profitability or entry barriers. In a general equilibrium context, even when there are no industry differences in profitability nor entry barriers, the model shows that there can be significant differences in equilibrium turnover rates due to differences in life-cycle dynamics. Following Greenwood, Zvi Hercowitz, and Per Krusell (1997) and Jason G. Cummins and Giovanni L. Violante (2002), ISTC is measured using the quality-adjusted relative price of capital used in each industry: however, these papers do not link ISTC to life-cycle dynamics. Jeffrey R. Campbell (1998) argues that ISTC may affect the cyclical behavior of aggregate entry and exit, and Klenow (1998) studies the cyclicality of investment in a related model. Samaniego (2008) finds that turnover and ISTC are positively related in a calibrated one-sector general equilibrium model.

### 60. aer.100.1.164.pdf

- PDF：[aer.100.1.164.pdf.pdf](./aer.100.1.164.pdf.pdf)

**同段完整语句：**

For most of the paper, entry, exit, and turnover are average annual rates over the sample period for each country-industry pair, to abstract from short-term conditions and from possible delays in the reporting of entry and exit. The measure of ISTC is the annual rate of decline in the quality-adjusted price of capital goods used by each industry, as measured in the United States. Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997) and Cummins and Violante (2002) show that, in a competitive environment with similar Cobb-Douglas production functions for different goods, a decline in the price of one good compared to another reflects an improvement in the productivity with which the first good is produced relative to the second. Cummins and Violante (2002) provide annual quality-adjusted price series for 26 types of equipment. These prices are divided by the official consumption and services deflator for each year, so that all capital goods prices are expressed relative to the price of nondurables.

Definition 2: A stationary equilibrium or balanced growth path (BGP) is a measure μ*, a mass of entrants εj* for each industry, and time paths for prices pjt such that the labor market clears, the measure replicates itself, all households maximize (4) subject to (5) given prices and expectations, and aggregate output yt grows at a constant rate. This definition is similar to that in Hopenhayn and Rogerson (1993), except that this model distinguishes between industries. Also, because rates of investment-specific and disembodied technical change differ across industries, relative prices will diverge along a balanced growth path, as in Greenwood et al. (1997). Proposition 1: There exists a unique balanced growth path with positive, constant rates of entry and exit into all sectors.

### 65. aer.100.2.73.pdf

- PDF：[aer.100.2.73.pdf.pdf](./aer.100.2.73.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：1
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Zvi Hercowitz and Per Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：investment, price, small, good, driven, output, derive, estimation, equation, open-economy

**同段完整语句：**

We derive the estimation equation from a small open-economy growth model which has two key features. First, the investment good is nontraded and produced from traded consumption good. Second, prices of investment are driven by exogenous changes in productivity in the investment sector, as in Jeremy Greenwood, Zvi Hercowitz, and Per Krusell (1997). These assumptions are motivated by the fact that imported investment goods account for a small share of aggregate investment expenditure. Moreover, the price of investment relative to output is volatile, and the volatility is by far driven by movements in the price of investment, not by those of output price.

### 66. aer.100.2.78.pdf

- PDF：[aer.100.2.78.pdf.pdf](./aer.100.2.78.pdf.pdf)

The Quantitative Role of Capital Goods Imports in US Growth By Michele Cavallo and Anthony Landry A significant body of literature has found that technological improvements embodied in new capital goods account for a large share of US output growth. This phenomenon, known as investment-specific technological change, has stimulated the growth rate of output by raising the efficiency of equipment and software (E&S) in the production of final output. In an influential contribution, Jeremy Greenwood, Zvi Hercowitz, and Per Krusell (1997) found that investment-specific technological change accounted for nearly 60 percent of growth in US output per hour during the postwar period. A notable fact is that an increasing share of US aggregate E&S investment expenditure has been allocated to capital goods imports. While capital goods imports were only 3.5 percent of E&S investment in 1967, by 2008 their share had risen tenfold to 36 percent.

### 68. aer.100.3.1214.pdf

- PDF：[aer.100.3.1214.pdf.pdf](./aer.100.3.1214.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：20
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Zvi Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：capital, price, investment, good, would, productivity, matches, around, intensity, same

**同段完整语句：**

In their paper, there is no heterogeneity in the productivity of matches (that is the capital intensity chosen is the same in all matches), but the price at which the capital is bought for the match depends on the prevailing investment good price. In contrast, I assumed that the money spent on capital is constant each period, so the interpretation would be that capital intensities in matches are different because the capital intensity would be inversely related to the price of capital. This would imply different labor productivities across cohorts. The volatility of the investment good price they use (following Jeremy Greenwood, Zvi Hercowitz, and Krusell 1997; and Jason J. Cummins and Violante 2002) is around the same as the volatility of the aggregate shock. A percentage change in the investment good price would imply around a third as much change in embodied productivity because the share of capital good in the production function is one-third. So if embodied productivity changes are to be driven by only investment technology shocks, they seem to explain around a third of unemployment fluctuations.

In this section, we suggest two interpretations for these shocks and rely on evidence outside our DSGE model to argue for the plausibility of both views. A. Investment-Specific Technology Shocks and the Relative Price of Investment A strict, model-based interpretation indicates that the investment shocks correspond either to investment-specific technological disturbances or, equivalently, to shocks to the relative price of investment in terms of consumption goods. In recent years, data on the latter have been used by other authors to proxy for investment-specific technology shocks [see, for instance, Greenwood et al. 1997, 2000; and Fisher 2006]. However, this relative price is not used in our estimation, as we also wish to consider other possible interpretations of the investment shock. More precisely, we fix the volatility of each shock to the average of the time-varying standard deviation for all four quarters in 1980.

If we subscribe to this broader interpretation of this disturbance—which is admittedly outside our current DSGE model—a natural explanation of the Great Moderation would also be based on a reduction in financial frictions. Interestingly, this purely "theoretical" hypothesis squares remarkably well with the empirical and anecdotal evidence about the expanded access to credit and borrowing for firms. This assumption allows us to directly compare our results to a large literature on Bayesian estimation of DSGE models [see, for instance, Levin et al. 2005; Del Negro et al. 2007; or Smets and Wouters 2007]. Assuming, instead, a nonstationary investment shock and using data on the relative price of investment in the estimation would require at least two important modifications: first, we would need to deflate all real variables by the consumption deflator [see Greenwood et al. 1997 or Fisher 2006], which would then become our measure of price inflation, providing perhaps a less accurate characterization of monetary policy in the Taylor rule; second, we would need some additional structural shocks or measurement errors for the observable variables [to avoid stochastic singularity]. We leave this extension for future work. The intuitive link between our shock to the relative price of investment and financial frictions is even more evident in models that take into consideration agency costs for the financing of investment, such as that of Charles T. Carlstrom and Timothy S. Fuerst (1997).

### 77. apel.12301.pdf

- PDF：[apel.12301.pdf.pdf](./apel.12301.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：投资特定技术冲击 / 商业周期
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：energy, capital, price-investment, different, response, rising, prices, channel, vintage, soes

**同段完整语句：**

In response to rising energy prices, SOEs tend to invest in energy-saving capital, which leads to lower energy intensity. This price-investment channel is less robust in NSOEs and FFEs. This price-investment channel is a manifestation of the vintage effect in capital. In the literature on vintage capital (see Solow 1962; Greenwood et al. 1997; Gilchrist and Williams 2000; Boucekkine et al. 2006, among many others), investments made at different times are embodied with different technology or associated with different productivity. Atkeson and Kehoe (1999) and Wei (2003) are two seminal papers that formalise the energy price-investment mechanism using dynamic stochastic general equilibrium (DSGE) models, calibrated on the US economy. In response to rising energy prices, firms choose energy-efficient machines and equipment, whose energy use per capita is low, to save energy expenditure.

- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：skill, capital, labor, katz, others, increase, premium, sbtc, autor, among

**同段完整语句：**

Still, the majority of previous work attributes the increase in the skill premium to SBTC. In empirical, mostly labor oriented, studies [e.g., Goldin and Katz (2007), Autor, Katz, and Kearney (2008), among others, Katz and Autor (1999) provide an overview], the change in labor demand is usually represented by a time trend that does not distinguish between changes in technology and changes in the allocation of capital. These shifts of labor demand can explain much of the evolution of the skill premium. While the shifts are usually attributed to SBTC, it is equally plausible to interpret them as an increase in skilled capital relative to unskilled capital. In theoretical models capital is included explicitly, but either differentiated along a different dimension than "use by skill level" [e.g., equipment and structures as in Krusell et al. (2000) and Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997), among others] or assuming identical production functions for all sectors (Caselli (1999), Galor and Moav (2000), Acemoglu (2002a), and others). While the latter is a common assumption, it is not a priori certain that it should hold in this case. The sectors of production in my model are differentiated with regard to the skill level of the workforce.

Summing-up, R&D and ETC are the main drivers of technological progress, with the former more related to product innovation and the latter more related to process innovation; obviously enough, the distinction between product and process innovation is often ambiguous from an empirical point of view (see, for instance, the diffusion of computers and telecommunication devices) and in many cases the two forms of innovation are strictly interrelated.

**同段完整语句：**

Here $q_t$ represents the state of the technology for producing physical capital, and it determines the amount of capital that can be purchased with one unit of consumption good. Hence $1/q_t$ is the relative price of physical capital in terms of the consumption good. An alternative formulation of the environment with declining relative price of equipment has been developed by Greenwood et al. (1997). In this formulation, the relative price of capital equipment is constant but its productivity is increasing over time. Using transformed variables, the law of motion for capital equipment and the production function is given by

$$
\tilde{K}_{t+1} = (1 - \delta) \tilde{K}_t, \quad \tilde{K}_t = q_{t-1} K_t
$$

where $q_{t-1}$ is the inverse relative price of capital equipment and $K_t$ is the physical capital stock.

### 95. Casey 等 2024Understanding climate damages Consumption versus investment

- PDF：[Casey 等_2024Understanding climate damages Consumption versus investment.pdf](./Casey%20等_2024Understanding%20climate%20damages%20Consumption%20versus%20investment.pdf)
- 页码：1
- 类型：投资特定技术冲击 / 商业周期
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：climate, change, productivity, investment, consumption, firms, goods, services, producing, produce

**同段完整语句：**

Introduction Climate change affects the productivity of firms producing investment goods and services differently from the productivity of firms producing consumption goods and services. For example, construction firms produce investment goods and are more vulnerable to climate change than retail firms, which primarily produce consumption services. A long literature shows that distinguishing between consumption and investment productivity has important implications for understanding economic growth (e.g., Greenwood et al., 1997; Grossman et al., 2017), comparative development (e.g., Hsieh and Klenow, 2007, 2010), trends in inequality (e.g., Krusell et al., 2000; Grossman et al., 2021), and business cycles (e.g., Fisher, 2006; Justiniano et al., 2010). However, the existing macro literature on climate change abstracts from this distinction and instead uses aggregate damage functions that assume climate change has equal impacts on consumption and investment productivity (e.g., Nordhaus and Boyer, 2003; Golosov et al., 2014; Hassler et al., 2016, 2021; Barrage, 2020; Barrage and Nordhaus, 2023). We develop a dynamic general equilibrium framework that allows climate change to have different effects on consumption and investment productivity.

### 96. coep.12152.pdf

- PDF：[coep.12152.pdf.pdf](./coep.12152.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献

**同段完整语句：**

In fact, recent empirical studies confirm that a large proportion of TFP growth is explained by embodied technical progress. For example, Castiglionesi and Ornaghi (2013) showed that TFP growth is driven entirely by embodied technical progress for Spanish manufacturing firms. Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997) reported investment-specific technical change accounts for approximately 60% of the postwar productivity growth of the United States. Tokui, Inui, and Kim (2008) suggested that embodied technical change would reduce TFP growth by about 0.4%–0.8% for the Japanese manufacturing industry for the period 1997–2002. These studies underscore the importance of an empirical framework that can capture the influence of embodied technical change when investigating the sources of TFP growth.

(1997) proposed a simple two-sector optimal growth model with investment-specific technical change where productivity grows faster in the investment than in the consumption sector, causing relative prices to change accordingly. In this new class of models different components of output grow at different rates, raising the issue of aggregation as in actual data. Section 2 uses the general methodology suggested in this paper to measure output growth in the two-sector AK model proposed by Rebelo (1991).

### 101. Durán和Licandro 2024Is the output growth rate in NIPA a welfare measure

- PDF：[Durán和Licandro_2024Is the output growth rate in NIPA a welfare measure.pdf](./Durán和Licandro_2024Is%20the%20output%20growth%20rate%20in%20NIPA%20a%20welfare%20measure.pdf)

**同段完整语句：**

With the introduction in NIPA of constant quality price indexes for equipment investment, two related new facts emerged. First, the price of equipment investment permanently declines relative to the price of non-durable consumption, and second, equipment investment permanently grows faster than non-durable consumption, implying that the investment-to-output ratio is permanently growing. To accommodate growth theory to these new facts, Greenwood et al. (1997), in their seminal paper, extended the neoclassical growth model to a two-sector (consumption and investment) growth model with two sources of technical progress, consumption- and investment-specific technical change; the latter interpreted as embodied in capital goods. 2 to show that the BEA had good fundamental reasons to use a Fisher ideal chain index to measure output growth.

### 102. Durán和Licandro 2024Is the output growth rate in NIPA a welfare measure

- PDF：[Durán和Licandro_2024Is the output growth rate in NIPA a welfare measure.pdf](./Durán和Licandro_2024Is%20the%20output%20growth%20rate%20in%20NIPA%20a%20welfare%20measure.pdf)

**同段完整语句：**

This section describes a simple version of the two-sector AK model proposed by Rebelo (1991) and applies to it the Fisher–Shell index proposed in Section 1.2 to show that the BEA had good fundamental reasons to use a Fisher ideal chain index to measure output growth. As shown by Felbermayr and Licandro (2005), the two-sector AK model is the simplest endogenous growth model that replicates the observed permanent decline in the relative price of equipment and the permanent increase in the investment-to-output ratio. We decided to use it instead of the original Greenwood et al. (1997) model, since the AK model has the advantage of jumping to the balanced growth path at the initial time, which allows for an explicit solution of the value function. This will help in illustrating the role of the money metric utility and comparing it to consumption-equivalent measures.

### 106. eca.2000.0008.pdf

- PDF：[eca.2000.0008.pdf.pdf](./eca.2000.0008.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：54
- 类型：一般理论依据
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：difficult, envision, technology, steadily, worsening, period, nearly, forty, years, estimates

**同段完整语句：**

Productivity growth in IT provides a final perspective on the conclusions of Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell and of Hercowitz. They argue that some 60 percent of postwar U.S. growth can be attributed to investment-specific (embodied) productivity growth, which they distinguish from input accumulation and (disembodied) productivity growth. As evidence, they note that the relative price of equipment in the United States has fallen 3 percent per year, which they interpret as evidence of technical change that affects capital goods but not consumption goods. Our decomposition, however, reveals that declines in the prices of investment goods are the consequence of improvements in industry (disembodied) productivity. Domar aggregation shows how these improvements contribute directly to aggregate TFP growth. There is no separate role for investment-specific technical change.

### 107. eca.2013.0016.pdf

- PDF：[eca.2013.0016.pdf.pdf](./eca.2013.0016.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：28
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：neoclassical, capital, through, technical, labor, share, theory, suggests, potential, sources

**同段完整语句：**

Neoclassical theory suggests two potential sources for capital deepening of this sort. The first is through capital-augmenting technical progress—that is, if AK in the above notation grows over time. A second channel is through investment-specific technical change driven by reductions in the relative price of investment associated with efficiency gains in the production of new capital goods (Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell 1997). Karabarbounis and Neiman (2013) highlight the latter as a particularly promising candidate explanation for the decline in labor's share. A great virtue of the simple neoclassical framework is that it delivers a rich set of empirical predictions on the joint evolution of labor's share, factor prices, and productivity.

Capital and labor can be reallocated frictionlessly across firms at the beginning of each period after the shocks $X$ and $y$ have been realized. Given the constant-return-to-scale technology, firms then face a constant (common) marginal cost.

### 109. ecca.12279.pdf

- PDF：[ecca.12279.pdf.pdf](./ecca.12279.pdf.pdf)

Therefore the economic depreciation rate of capital is approximately equal to the sum of the physical depreciation rate dk and the obsolescence rate cp, which is equal to the rate of decline in the relative price of investment and, under perfect competition, equals the rate of investment-specific technical progress. As Greenwood et al. (1997, app. B) note: 'In a world with investment-specific technological change, the rate of economic depreciation exceeds the rate of physical depreciation due to the fact that this form of technological change obsoletes the old capital stock.' 10.

### 110. ecca.12332.pdf

- PDF：[ecca.12332.pdf.pdf](./ecca.12332.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：1
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：countries, equipment, capital, erences, trade, country, percentile, income, higher, mutreja

**同段完整语句：**

INTRODUCTION The capital per worker in a country at the 90th percentile of the world income distribution is about 75 times higher than in a country at the 10th percentile (Mutreja 2014). Less developed countries also have a substantially higher proportion of their total capital stock in structures, while richer countries are more heavily invested in equipment goods. Given that a well-documented growth literature has shown equipment goods to be 'carriers' of new technology and catalysts for economic growth (Cairncross 1961; DeLong and Summers 1991, 1993; Jones 1994; Lee 1995; Greenwood et al. 1997; Mazumdar 2001), several papers document that high relative capital (and equipment) prices help to explain income differences across countries (Mutreja et al. 2018; Armenter and Amartyr 2012; Hsieh and Klenow 2007; Eaton and Kortum 2001; Restuccia and Urrutia 2001). What remain unclear are the factors and mechanisms that can lead to differences in equipment prices. Our paper contributes to the literature by empirically identifying and measuring the extent to which countries' trade openness—and conversely, actions that can constrain trade channels or distort trade—is associated with relative equipment price differences across developing countries.

### 111. ecca.12332.pdf

- PDF：[ecca.12332.pdf.pdf](./ecca.12332.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：6
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：equipment, trade, prices, relative, countries, goods, therefore, likely, emerging, open

**同段完整语句：**

Countries that are more open to free trade are expected to exchange a greater proportion of their goods and therefore are more likely to compete on prices in the world market. The degree of bilateral trade between emerging and developed economies can also be an important indicator of the emerging economy's ability to acquire equipment goods at lower relative costs. For example, Greenwood et al. (1997) show that relative equipment prices have steadily declined in the USA as technological advances have made equipment less expensive. Therefore developing countries that trade more with technologically advanced nations are more likely to observe reductions in their relative equipment prices.

In future work, it would be also interesting to further investigate which channel may be responsible for these high social returns to physical capital leading to positive long-run growth effects. Some of these channels imply the existence of learning by doing processes in the accumulation of physical capital as in Arrow (1962), the presence of positive externalities to the accumulation of productive capital (Romer 1986), the process of technological transfer through trade of capital goods across countries (Eaton and Kortum 2001), and the embodiment of technological progress in new vintages of capital (Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell 1997).

### 114. ecin.12062.pdf

- PDF：[ecin.12062.pdf.pdf](./ecin.12062.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：11
- 类型：校准 / 参数取值
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：economy, share, capital, data, factor, equipment, structures, imply, valentinyi, herrendorf

**同段完整语句：**

Using data on the U.S. economy, Valentinyi and Herrendorf (2008) measure the factor share of land, equipment capital, and structures capital at the sectoral level. Their measures for the aggregate economy (and, also, for nonagriculture) imply a $\mu$ of 0.54. Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997) calibrate a model of investment-specific technological change to data on the U.S. economy and their estimates imply an equipment factor share of 0.56. Also, Krusell et al. (2000) build a quantitative model of capital-skill complementarity and estimate an income share of structures capital of 0.117. This corresponds to $(1 - \mu)\alpha$ in my article, implying a $\mu$ of 0.65.

### 119. Macroeconomic Implications of Agglomeration

- PDF：[ECTA9029.pdf.pdf](./ECTA9029.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：Economic growth, productivity, increasing returns, agglomeration, density

**同段完整语句：**

With a positive trend in land prices, agglomeration affects growth via two channels. First, firms economize on land when it becomes more costly, thereby increasing congestion and lowering growth. This effect is analogous, though opposite in direction, to the effect on capital of falling equipment prices in Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997). Second, when rising land prices curtail land use, density and, therefore, TFP grow faster than they would otherwise. We estimate that land prices indeed have a positive secular trend, growing 1.0% per year between 1978 and 2009.

### 120. Macroeconomic Implications of Agglomeration

- PDF：[ECTA9029.pdf.pdf](./ECTA9029.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：9
- 类型：校准 / 参数取值
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：Economic growth, productivity, increasing returns, agglomeration, density

**同段完整语句：**

The parameter $\gamma_j > 0$ is the growth rate of the technology for producing the j-type investment good relative to that for consumption. If $\gamma_j \neq 1$, the corresponding investment technology exhibits a trend. We consider trends in the investment technologies because they exist empirically and, similar to Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997), they influence our estimates. We also allow for growth in the Hicks-neutral technology and the number of households $N_t$, given by $\gamma_a > 0$ and $\gamma_n > 0$. Along the balanced growth path, the average growth of city-specific output equals the constant rate of aggregate output growth.

### 126. icc%252Fdty001.pdf

- PDF：[icc%252Fdty001.pdf.pdf](./icc%252Fdty001.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：5
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：innovation, vivarelli, process, firms, product, conte, introducing, other, related, investment

**同段完整语句：**

However, the innovation literature suggests that it is product innovation which is significantly based on formal R&D: for instance Parisi et al. (2006) and Conte and Vivarelli (2014) found robust and significant evidence that R&D increases the likelihood of introducing product innovation. On the other hand, process innovation is much more related to ETC acquired by investment in new machinery and equipment (see Freeman et al., 1982). Indeed, the embodied nature of technological progress and the effects related to its spread in the economy were originally theoretically discussed by Salter (1960) (see also Solow, 1960; Jorgenson, 1966); later, vintage capital models have been put forward to describe how the replacement of old equipment is the main way through which firms introduce process innovation (see Clark, 1987; Hulten, 1992; Greenwood et al., 1997; Hercowitz, 1998; Mukoyama, 2006). In other words, while R&D is the main vehicle for introducing disembodied knowledge, innovative investment and updated scrapping are the ways how firms introduce more advanced process innovation. Moreover, sectoral and microeconomic studies show that R&D is crucial in large firms and more advanced sectors, while ETC assumes a dominant role in SMEs, more traditional sectors, and developing countries (see Pavitt, 1984; Acs and Audretsch 1990; Audretsch and Vivarelli, 1996; Brouwer and Kleinknecht, 1996; Conte and Vivarelli, 2014; Haile et al., 2017).

The focus of this article is on investment-sector efficiency shocks, their effects, and the implications of capturing them with MFP shocks or with MEI shocks. ### 135. iere.12075.pdf

- PDF：[iere.12075.pdf.pdf](./iere.12075.pdf.pdf)

(1997) and Oulton (2007) assume that (using our terminology) assembly is completely specialized and that investment adjustment is costless.

### 136. iere.12075.pdf

- PDF：[iere.12075.pdf.pdf](./iere.12075.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：10
- 类型：投资特定技术冲击 / 商业周期
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：baseline, calibration, equivalence, parameter, choices, shocks, share, equipment, structures, investment

**同段完整语句：**

Baseline Calibration Ensuring Equivalence. Table 3 summarizes the parameter choices for a baseline calibration that we use to illustrate aggregate equivalence (AE) between MEI and MFP shocks under our extended conditions. To facilitate comparisons with previous work on MEI shocks, we adhere to the parameter choices of Greenwood et al. (1997) whenever possible. Accordingly, the output share of equipment in both the M and N sectors is 17% and the share of structures is 13%. The parameters governing the assembly functions are set so that there is complete specialization: consumption and structures investment are assembled using inputs from the N sector only, whereas equipment investment is assembled using inputs from the M sector only.

### 137. iere.12075.pdf

- PDF：[iere.12075.pdf.pdf](./iere.12075.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：10
- 类型：文献定位 / 简短引用
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：when, capital, conjecture, there, factors, production, sufficient, factor, mobile, example

**同段完整语句：**

We conjecture that, when there are two or more factors of production, it is sufficient for all but one factor to be mobile. For example, see Sargent (1987) for a case of an immobile capital stock when one good is produced by multiple firms. For simplicity, we abstract from trend growth as well as capital and labor taxes, whereas Greenwood et al. (1997) incorporate them in their model. The substitution elasticities between inputs in assembly become irrelevant under complete specialization.

### 140. iere.12075.pdf

- PDF：[iere.12075.pdf.pdf](./iere.12075.pdf.pdf)

(1997), the baseline calibration implies identical production functions across sectors. However, for the three factor inputs in the model, U.S. data imply different input intensities across the machinery and non-machinery sectors (the M and N sectors in the model). To differentiate the intensities of factor inputs across sectors, we used the following restrictions: (a) while allowing variation across sectors, we kept the aggregate factor input intensities the same as in Greenwood et al. (1997); (b) factor payments are equalized across sectors, making the factors' shares of sectoral output proportional to the sectoral stocks of capital (since production functions are Cobb-Douglas); (c) factor input intensities are equal regardless of where the output of a sector is used.

### 145. j.1365-2966.2007.00425.x.pdf

**同段完整语句：**

In this paper we focus on one such factor, investment-specific productivity shocks. A series of recent papers have investigated, mostly in a closed-economy context, the importance of investment-specific technological changes in accounting for growth and business cycle properties of output. Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997) find that investment-specific technological changes explain approximately 60% of growth in output per man-hour in post-war U.S. data. Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (2000) set up a closed-economy business cycle model where business cycle fluctuations are produced by investment-specific technological changes. They calibrate their model to the U.S. economy and find that these changes explain approximately 30% of the variation in output.

### 147. j.1365-2966.2007.00450.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1365-2966.2007.00450.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1365-2966.2007.00450.x.pdf.pdf)

- 关键词：price, capital, goods, technological, displays, trend, growth, economy, change, relative

**同段完整语句：**

(F5) The price of new capital goods relative to the price of consumption goods displays a downward trend (Gordon 1990). (F6) The investment-to-output ratio ($Q_I/Y$) displays a positive trend. Greenwood, Hercowitz, and Krusell (1997, 2000) and Gort, Greenwood, and Rupert (1999) interpret the negative co-movement between the price and quantity of new capital (F5 and F6) as evidence that there has been significant technological progress in the production of capital goods. In fact, Greenwood et al. (1997) have found that in order to sustain growth in the long run the U.S. economy has relied on investment-specific technological change. In comparison, TFP growth (which they call residual-neutral technological change) had virtually no impact on the long-run performance of the U.S. economy, at least not since the mid-1970s.

### 153. j.1467-9361.2005.00299.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1467-9361.2005.00299.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1467-9361.2005.00299.x.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：5
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：capital, consumption, good, over, time, should, efficiency, units, price, effect

**同段完整语句：**

Since the capital goods are increasingly efficient over time, the marginal productivity of capital should incorporate this efficiency. It is expressed in efficiency units in equation (7), i.e., it is multiplied by $q_t$. On the other hand, it should be noted that, consistently with Greenwood et al. (1997), the price of the capital good in terms of the consumption good is $1/q_t$ in our model: For each unit of forgone consumption at t, the economy can build up $q_t$ units of capital at t. Suppose that $q_t$ is increasing, then the relative price of capital is decreasing, and the consumption good is expected to be more expensive over time, and consumption is likely to fall in the future. This effect is called obsolescence effect by Boucekkine et al. (2003); it is inherent to embodied technical change and it tends to lower the growth effects of the latter.

### 154. j.1467-937x.2007.00449.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1467-937x.2007.00449.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1467-937x.2007.00449.x.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：1
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：productivity, growth, over, past, technological, embodied, capital, especially, violante, change

**同段完整语句：**

INTRODUCTION Over the past three decades, the nature of growth and productivity advancement has gone through a profound transformation: technological innovations embodied in new and more productive capital goods—especially in information and communication equipment and software—have represented the major source of output growth in the U.S. and Europe (Jorgenson, 2001; Colecchia and Schreyer, 2002). Productivity growth embodied in new vintages of capital has accelerated significantly over the past 30 years, from 2% per year in the 1960's to 4·5% in the 1990's (Gordon, 1990; Cummins and Violante, 2002). As a result, the emphasis in growth-accounting exercises has moved from factor-neutral productivity to "investment-specific productivity" (Greenwood, Hercowitz and Krusell, 1997). How does technological change, especially in this form, influence labour-market outcomes? An extensive literature argues that this episode of capital-embodied technical change has a "skillbiased" character, whereby the productivity of high-skilled workers has risen in relative terms with the arrival of new technologies (e.g. Katz and Murphy, 1992; Krusell, Ohanian, Ríos-Rull and Violante, 2000).

### 156. j.1467-937x.2007.00452.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1467-937x.2007.00452.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1467-937x.2007.00452.x.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：10
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood Hercowitz and Krusell 1997`
- 关键词：technology, leading, time, capital, probability, neutral, expected, value, will, unit

**同段完整语句：**

Formally, with probability $1 - a_z$ the current-period job's neutral technology, $z_{it}$, remains in expected value unchanged, so that $z_{it} = z_{it-1} + \varepsilon_{it}$, where $\varepsilon_{it}$ is an idiosyncratic shock which is iid normal with zero mean and standard deviation $\sigma$, while, with probability $a_z$, a job catches up with the leading technology in the economy and $z_{it} = z_t + \varepsilon_{it}$, so that the job technology equals (in expected value) the leading technology of that time, $z_t$. Here, we will refer to the difference between the leading technology $z_t$ and the job's neutral technology $z_{it}$ as the job technological gap, $\tau_{it} = z_t - z_{it}$. As in Solow (1960) and Greenwood, Hercowitz and Krusell (1997), the sector producing capital is perfectly competitive and at time $t$ can produce one unit of quality-adjusted capital at marginal cost $e^{-q_t}$, which will also be the price of a capital unit at that time.

The cumulative impact of each of the three effects is shown in Figure 8. An alternative formulation of the residual labor productivity hypothesis would be to allow for a trend in the efficiency of capital equipment. ### 160. j.1467-9485.2011.0569.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1467-9485.2011.0569.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1467-9485.2011.0569.x.pdf.pdf)

**同段完整语句：**

Further, Levine and Renelt (1992) have shown that the investment share is a robust variable in explaining economic growth. This positive and statistically significant effect of investment on the growth rate of countries suggests that investment not only affects the stock of physical capital but also increases intangible capital, such as knowledge, so that the social return to investment is larger than the private return. Cooley et al. (1997) and Greenwood et al. (1997) argue that investment in physical capital has a larger influence on economic growth than is suggested by the factor share. This relationship holds because technological improvements are incorporated in physical capital that are not reflected in the share paid to physical capital. For those reasons, building a theoretical model that relates positive externalities of investment to physical capital seems to be a reasonable approach. In this Study we intend to combine the two approaches mentioned above.

- 关键词：capital, goods, trade, technologies, total, foreign, productivity, growth, models, spillovers

**同段完整语句：**

In this paper, we argue that the total volume of trade as a measure of exposure to foreign technologies as an important source of productivity gains is not the most appropriate one. Rather, we focus on imports of research and development (R&D)-intensive capital goods to capture technology diffusion. In growth models without spillovers and where new technologies arise in new vintages of capital goods (Greenwood et al., 1997), trade gives access to foreign goods and implicitly to embodied technologies. In this case, trade in R&D-intensive goods brings about some benefits in the form of an increase in capital good's efficiency. Moreover, in endogenous growth models with knowledge spillovers (Grossman and Helpman, 1991; and Rivera-Batiz and Romer, 1991a and 1991b) trade in differentiated capital goods raises capital efficiency and total factor productivity through learning and imitation.

### 162. j.1467-9957.2003.00370.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1467-9957.2003.00370.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1467-9957.2003.00370.x.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：product, capital, goods, improvement, quality, price, technological, cant, economies, scale

**同段完整语句：**

Improvement of product quality plays an important role in reducing unit costs in the recent growth industries such as microelectronics, semiconductors and telecommunications, as indicated by Sengupta (2000). For example, Hulten (1992) and Greenwood et al. (1997) estimated a positive macroeconomic impact of quality improvement through capital goods on efficiency and showed that capital goods of newer vintages have led to a steady decline in the relative price of capital goods. As Greenwood et al. (1997) stated, the negative comovement between price and quantity can be interpreted as evidence that there exists a significant technological change in the production of new product. Hence, technological advances have made new product less expensive.

### 164. j.1467-9957.2005.00427.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1467-9957.2005.00427.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1467-9957.2005.00427.x.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：2
- 类型：长期增长核算 / TFP 贡献
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：investment, equipment, returns, often, technological, progress, embodied, machinery, oecd, countries

**同段完整语句：**

Overall, these findings point to the DS results being suggestive only, and that the returns to investment in machinery and equipment are imprecise, and often small, for the OECD countries. However, one may question the finding of Auerbach et al. (1994), amongst others, that the social returns to investment in machinery and equipment are below the private returns in the OECD countries. Assuming nonnegative externalities to investment, this evidence is hard to reconcile with the fact that private firms invest even if the returns to their investment do not exceed the cost of capital. Furthermore, investment in equipment is often associated with embodied technological progress, which has been stressed as an important engine of labour productivity growth (Hulten, 1975, 1992; Greenwood et al., 1997; Gordon, 2003). Greenwood et al. (1997) find that a large fraction of total factor productivity growth in the USA can be attributed to embodied technological progress and they find a significant positive correlation between embodied technological progress and investment in equipment. In fact, technological progress often forces firms to undertake investment in technologically more advanced equipment along with investment in, often unmeasured, complementary capital stock.

- 关键词：investment, where, real, rate, prices, equipment, depreciation, tangible, capital, stock

**同段完整语句：**

where $r$ is the real interest rate or the real required return to equity, $d_T$ is the depreciation rate for the tangible capital stock, $d_I$ is the depreciation rate for the intangible capital stock, $\phi_I$ and $\phi_T$ are real prices of investment in intangibles and tangibles, respectively. Meanwhile, $\phi_T = P_T / P_O$, where $P_T$ is the price of investment in tangibles and $P_O$ reflects output prices, $\phi_I = P_I / P_O$, where $P_I$ is the price of R&D equipment, or, more generally, intangibles, and a dot over a variable signifies the time derivative. Embodied technological progress is represented by the $(\phi_I, \phi_T)$ terms that reflect the current state of the technology for producing tangible and intangible investment goods (Greenwood et al., 1997). The terms determine the amount of computers, machinery, software, information technology equipment and communication equipment that can be purchased for one unit of output. They thus play an important role in capturing effects of technological revolutions that are usually characterised by reductions in prices of investment goods (Perez, 2002; Gordon, 2003; Jovanovic and Rousseau, 2003).

### 173. j.1468-0297.2009.02280.x.pdf

**同段完整语句：**

Technical change embodied in new capital goods is captured by our measure of capital input through the use of quality-adjusted prices and user costs as weights in asset aggregation. In addition, one might also be interested in a proxy for embodied technological change. One way to address this is by measuring capital input as the capital stock deflated at real acquisition prices and aggregated with nominal asset shares (Greenwood et al., 1997). The difference between the EU KLEMS capital input series and this new series would be a proxy for embodied technological change. The EU KLEMS database provides the basic investment and capital stocks series to construct alternative measures of capital input.

### 176. j.1468-0335.2009.00817.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1468-0335.2009.00817.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1468-0335.2009.00817.x.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：1
- 类型：资本体现型技术 / vintage
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：progress, assumption, balanced, growth, technological, however, rate, empirical, kinds, under

**同段完整语句：**

The standard way to introduce balanced growth in macroeconomic models is to assume labour-augmenting technological progress (see, for example, King et al. 1988). However, this assumption is not sufficient for our purpose since it implies that all variables (except labour) grow at the same rate, which does not agree with the empirical facts listed above. As shown in Greenwood et al. (1997), it is possible to account for the empirical observation that equipment grows at a higher rate than output by introducing two other kinds of technological progress, such as equipment-specific and Hicks-neutral ones. However, these two kinds of progress alone are consistent with balanced growth only under the assumption of the Cobb-Douglas production function (see Greenwood et al. 1997, p. 347) and not under our assumption of the CES production function.

- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：assumption, production, function, however, rate, empirical, kinds, progress, consistent, balanced

**同段完整语句：**

However, this assumption is not sufficient for our purpose since it implies that all variables (except labour) grow at the same rate, which does not agree with the empirical facts listed above. As shown in Greenwood et al. (1997), it is possible to account for the empirical observation that equipment grows at a higher rate than output by introducing two other kinds of technological progress, such as equipment-specific and Hicks-neutral ones. However, these two kinds of progress alone are consistent with balanced growth only under the assumption of the Cobb-Douglas production function (see Greenwood et al. 1997, p. 347) and not under our assumption of the CES production function. The main theoretical result of the present paper is that we can make the CES production function consistent with balanced growth by combining the standard labour-augmenting technological progress with two kinds of progress introduced in Greenwood et al. (1997).

### 181. j.1468-0351.2006.00263.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1468-0351.2006.00263.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1468-0351.2006.00263.x.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：12
- 类型：测量 ISTC / 相对价格
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：relative, productivity, example, improving, home, producers, good, models, quality, respect

**同段完整语句：**

For example, improving the relative productivity of home producers of the $i$th good with respect to foreign producers of the $j$th good would in most models lead to increases in both $q_{ij}$ and $\tilde{q}_{ij}$ due to a declining relative price of home products. This standard result is implied, for example, by the dynamic Ricardian model of the terms of trade exposed in Obstfeld and Rogoff (1996). It is also a direct consequence of extended two-sector growth models with different productivity improvements across sectors, such as in Greenwood et al. (1997) or Whelan (2003). Indeed, it is in obvious conflict with the notion of productivity convergence of transition countries and with the observed trends of real appreciation in tradables. Therefore, it appears that productivity effects are more than offset by improving relative quality of home- and foreign-produced goods, which arises when relative quality is not sufficiently accounted for by statistical offices.

### 184. j.1468-2354.2011.00678.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1468-2354.2011.00678.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1468-2354.2011.00678.x.pdf.pdf)
- 页码：1
- 类型：投资特定技术冲击 / 商业周期
- 命中短语：`Greenwood et al 1997`
- 关键词：labor, market, theoretical, analysis, enable, scheme, shocks, frictions, technological, progress

**同段完整语句：**

The addition of these two features is motivated by their empirical relevance and theoretical appeal. Moreover, importantly for the analysis of this article, as detailed below, they enable a new scheme to identify neutral technology shocks. Empirically, Rogerson and Shimer (2010) show that labor markets are characterized by frictions that prevent the competitive market mechanism from determining labor market equilibrium allocations, thereby suggesting that their presence is important for a realistic description of the functioning of the labor market. Additionally, the analysis by Greenwood et al. (1997), Fisher (2006), and Justiniano et al. (2010) points out that the inclusion of investment-specific technological progress is key to study the dynamics of the technological progress. Theoretically, labor market frictions introduce the extensive margin of labor (i.e., (un)employment) into the model, whereas this dimension is absent in standard models of the labor market. In this way, the theoretical framework is able to detail the dynamics of hiring and labor market tightness—defined as the ratio between hiring and unemployment—whose reactions to shocks enable a new, agnostic, identification scheme that holds across models and is robust to plausible parameterizations.

The model economy consists of a representative household, a representative goods-producing firm, a continuum of intermediategoods-producing firms indexed by i ∈ [0, 1], and a central bank. The labor market is based on the assumption that the processes of job search and recruitment are costly for both the firm and worker.

- 关键词：shock, positive, neutral, technology, variables, both, response, hiring, illustrate, theoretical

**同段完整语句：**

To illustrate how the variables of the theoretical model react to each shock, Figures 1 and 2 plot impulse responses of variables to one positive percentage-point deviation of neutral and investment-specific technology shock for the model with flexible and staggered price setting, respectively. Independently from the shock considered, capital and investment show similar dynamics, as they both rise. In addition, the long-run response of output is positive for both shocks, although the impact response is more pronounced in the case of a neutral technology shock, which corroborates the findings in Greenwood et al. (1997) and Fisher (2006). The reactions of consumption, hiring, labor market tightness, and the cost of hiring to a neutral technology shock are positive. The intuition for these results is straightforward.

### 189. j.1475-3995.2009.00747.x.pdf

- PDF：[j.1475-3995.2009.00747.x.pdf.pdf](./j.1475-3995.2009.00747.x.pdf.pdf)
